# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Overview

**Task ID**: c_api_graphql_expert_079_architectural_understanding_expert_01
**Category**: architectural_understanding
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: c
**Context Length**: 1002187 tokens
**Files**: 84

## Task Title

Architectural Migration Plan: Custom IPC to gRPC

## Description

The SynestheticCanvas API Suite is a high-performance, C-based microservices system. It currently uses a proprietary, low-level Inter-Process Communication (IPC) library, `sc_ipc`, for communication between the API Gateway and the backend microservices (`palette`, `texture`, `audio`, `narrative`). While this custom solution was performant for the initial design, it has become a maintenance burden and hinders plans to introduce new services written in other languages. The engineering leadership is evaluating a migration to gRPC for its standardized interface definition, cross-language support, and robust ecosystem. This task requires a deep architectural analysis of the existing system to produce a high-level migration plan.

## Your Task

You are a principal engineer tasked with evaluating the feasibility of migrating the SynestheticCanvas suite from its custom IPC mechanism to gRPC. Your analysis must be based on the provided file system.

Your deliverable is a technical report that addresses the following points:

1.  **Component Identification:** Identify and list all the specific files and modules across the entire codebase that constitute the current inter-service communication system. This includes the client-side implementation in the API Gateway, the server-side implementation in the microservices, and the shared library itself.

2.  **Data Flow Analysis:** Based on the code and documentation (especially `docs/architecture/data_flow.puml`), describe the end-to-end flow of a request from the API Gateway to a backend microservice (e.g., `texture-service`) and back. Detail the key functions, data structures, and libraries involved in this communication path.

3.  **Migration Strategy Proposal:** Outline a high-level, phased plan to migrate the `texture-service` and the API Gateway's communication with it to gRPC. Your plan must address:
    *   The necessary code and build system modifications (e.g., `CMakeLists.txt`) for both the API Gateway and the `texture-service`.
    *   A strategy for managing the transition to minimize or eliminate service downtime. How can the system operate with a mix of old and new IPC mechanisms simultaneously?
    *   A description of what the new gRPC-based communication flow would look like.

4.  **Risk Assessment:** Identify and explain the top 3-5 technical risks and challenges associated with this migration. Consider factors beyond just code changes, such as build complexity, performance characteristics, deployment, and operational management.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this task by systematically dissecting the architecture from multiple angles:

1.  **Top-Down Analysis:** Start with the documentation, specifically `docs/architecture/overview.md`, `docs/architecture/microservices.md`, and `docs/architecture/data_flow.puml`, to build a mental model of the system's components and their interactions.

2.  **Code-Level Investigation:**
    *   Identify the core IPC library, which is clearly `libs/sc_ipc/`. Analyze `sc_ipc.c` and its header to understand its API (e.g., functions for connecting, sending, receiving).
    *   Locate the client-side usage. A search for `sc_ipc` functions would lead to `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c`. This file is the linchpin for how the gateway communicates with all backend services.
    *   Locate the server-side usage. The `main.c` file for each microservice (e.g., `services/texture-service/src/main.c`) is the most likely place to find the server-side IPC initialization and request-handling loop.

3.  **Synthesize and Plan:**
    *   Trace a full request path: A GraphQL request hits a resolver in `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c`, which calls a function that uses the `service_client.c` to send a request via `sc_ipc`. The `texture-service`'s `main.c` receives this, passes it to `texture_handler.c`, which uses `texture_service.c` for business logic.
    *   For the migration plan, the expert would propose defining a `texture.proto` file for the gRPC service contract.
    *   They would suggest modifying the `CMakeLists.txt` for the gateway and the texture service to find and link the gRPC and Protobuf libraries.
    *   The core of the plan would involve a parallel deployment strategy. The `texture-service` would be modified to listen on two ports simultaneously: one for the old `sc_ipc` and one for the new `gRPC` server. The API Gateway's configuration (`sc_config`) would be extended to include a feature flag or a new service address, allowing it to select which protocol to use for the `texture-service`. This enables a gradual rollout without a "big bang" cutover.

4.  **Risk Identification:** The expert would think beyond the code and identify systemic risks: the complexity of adding gRPC's C++ dependencies to a C project's CMake build system, potential performance differences between a lean custom TCP protocol and HTTP/2-based gRPC, and the operational complexity of managing a hybrid-communication system during the transition period.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Component Identification Accuracy:** Did the agent correctly identify the key files (`service_client.c`, service `main.c` files, `sc_ipc.c`) responsible for the current IPC mechanism?
- **Architectural Flow Comprehension:** Was the agent able to accurately describe the request flow from the gateway to a microservice, referencing the correct modules (resolvers, service client, handlers)?
- **Migration Plan Viability:** Is the proposed migration plan technically sound and realistic? Does it include a phased rollout strategy (e.g., parallel systems) rather than a risky "big bang" approach?
- **Build & Dependency Awareness:** Did the agent recognize that modifying the `CMakeLists.txt` files and managing the gRPC/Protobuf dependencies is a non-trivial part of the task?
- **Risk Assessment Depth:** Did the agent identify sophisticated risks beyond simple coding errors, such as build system complexity, performance implications, and operational overhead during the transition?
- **Use of Evidence:** Does the agent's analysis refer to specific files, documentation (`data_flow.puml`), and architectural patterns to support its conclusions?

     1→/*
     2→ * SynestheticCanvas - API Gateway
     3→ * --------------------------------
     4→ * service_client.c
     5→ *
     6→ * A production-grade, thread-safe service client wrapper around libcurl that is
     7→ * responsible for communicating with downstream creative micro-services
     8→ * (palette, texture, audio, narrative).  The client provides:
     9→ *
    10→ *  • Configurable per-service base URLs loaded from environment variables
    11→ *  • Automatic request instrumentation (request / failure counters)
    12→ *  • Exponential-back-off retries with jitter
    13→ *  • JSON parsing (cJSON) and basic validation
    14→ *  • Centralised structured logging
    15→ *
    16→ * Author  : SynestheticCanvas Core Team
    17→ * License : MIT
    18→ */

     1→/*
     2→ * sc_ipc.h
     3→ * ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
     4→ * SynestheticCanvas Inter-Process Communication (IPC) library – Public API
     5→ *
     6→ * The IPC layer allows individual SynestheticCanvas micro-services to exchange
     7→ * strongly-typed messages with predictable latency guarantees.  The transport
     8→ * is based on UNIX domain sockets with configurable timeouts, automatic
     9→ * envelope framing, and correlation identifiers for request/response
    10→ * matching.  The ABI is stable and versioned; breaking changes will bump
    11→ * SC_IPC_VERSION_MAJOR.
    12→ *
    13→ * Copyright (c) 2024
    14→ *   SynestheticCanvas Contributors <oss@synestheticcanvas.io>

91-assistanttext-
I have completed the technical report for the gRPC migration plan. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary

The report at `/logs/agent/solution.md` addresses all four deliverables requested:

### 1. Component Identification
I identified that the SynestheticCanvas system uses a **hybrid communication approach**:
- The `sc_ipc` library (`libs/sc_ipc/`) provides UNIX domain socket IPC with length-prefixed framing
- The API Gateway uses `service_client.c` with libcurl for HTTP/REST calls to microservices
- Microservices expose HTTP endpoints via libmicrohttpd

Key files identified:
- `libs/sc_ipc/include/sc_ipc.h` and `src/sc_ipc.c` - IPC library
- `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` - HTTP client
- `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c` - GraphQL resolvers
- `services/texture-service/src/main.c` - Service entry point
- `services/texture-service/src/texture_handler.c` - Request handlers

### 2. Data Flow Analysis
Traced the complete request path from client through API Gateway to texture-service:
1. Client sends GraphQL/REST request to Gateway
2. Rate limiting and validation occurs
3. Resolver dispatches to `service_client.c`
4. HTTP request via libcurl to microservice
5. Microservice processes via libmicrohttpd router
6. Handler invokes business logic, returns JSON response

### 3. Migration Strategy
Proposed a 4-phase approach:
- **Phase 1**: Define `.proto` contracts, modify CMakeLists.txt for gRPC/Protobuf
- **Phase 2**: Implement dual-protocol support (HTTP + gRPC simultaneously)
- **Phase 3**: Gradual rollout via feature flags (5% → 100%)
- **Phase 4**: Consolidation - remove HTTP, move to gRPC-only

The key innovation is the **parallel deployment strategy** where services listen on both protocols simultaneously, controlled by environment variables like `SC_US
... (truncated)

Vision\n\nSynestheticCanvas transforms every HTTP or WebSocket request into a _brush-stroke_ on a living digital canvas.  \nMicroservices supply the colors, textures, and motion, while the **GraphQL/REST gateway** orchestrates them into a single, time-synchronous response.  \nThe architecture has three non-negotiable goals:\n\n1. **Expressiveness** \u2013 Artists can combine services like mixing paint.  \n2. **Evolution** \u2013 New art forms (e.g., volumetric audio) can be added without breaking existing exhibitions.  \n3. **Performance** \u2013 Frame-accurate (< 16 ms) responses even under festival-scale load.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Macro-Level Topology\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    subgraph Client Edge\n        VR[VR Headset]\n        Web[Web Frontend]\n        Bot[AI Bot]\n    end\n\n    subgraph Gateway Layer\n        GQL(GraphQL Gateway)\n        REST(REST Fallback)\n    end\n\n    subgraph Core Services\n        Palette(Palette Svc)\n        Synth(Texture Synth)\n        Audio(Audio-React)\n        Narr(Narrative Engine)\n    end\n    \n    subgraph Shared Infra\n        LogStack(ELK/OTel)\n        Redis((Redis Cache))\n        MQ((NATS JetStream))\n        PG[(PostgreSQL Cluster)]\n    end\n\n    VR -->|Query / Mutation| GQL\n    Web --> GQL\n    Bot --> REST\n    \n    GQL -- gRPC/json --> Palette & Synth & Audio & Narr\n    REST -- HTTP--> Palette & Synth & Audio & Narr\n    \n    GQL -- sub/ms logs --> LogStack\n    REST -- prometheus --> LogStack\n    \n    Palette --- PG\n    Synth --- Redis\n    Audio --- MQ\n    Narr  --- PG\n\n    classDef red fill:#ffdfe0,stroke:#ce2b37,stroke-width:2;\n    class REST red\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Layered Breakdown\n\n| Layer                | Responsibility                                           | Key Patterns                        |\n|----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------|\n| **Gateway**          | Auth, rate-limit, schema stitching, cache-aside          | API Gateway, GraphQL Schema         |\n| **Service Layer**    | Domain orchestrations, streaming, CQRS                   | Command/Query Separation            |\n| **Repository Layer** | Data access, DAO mapping, migrations                     | Repository Pattern                  |\n| **Infra**            | Observability, tracing, message bus, persistence         | Sidecar + 12-Factor                 |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Gateway Internals\n\n### 4.1 GraphQL Route Lifecycle\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant C as Client\n    participant G as Gateway\n    participant V as Validator\n    participant S as Service\n    participant L as Logger\n    \n    C->>G: gql { mutateTexture(...) }\n    G->>V: schema.validate(request)\n    V->>G: Ok / Err\n    alt Err\n        G->>C: 422 Unprocessable Entity\n        G->>L: warn(validation)\n    else Ok\n        G->>S: gRPC call (texture-synth)\n        S-->>G: TexturePayload\n        G->>L: info(request)\n        G->>C: 200 + JSON\n    end\n```\n\n#### 4.1.1 Validation Rules\n* **Static** \u2013 schema-compiled (enum ranges, non-null fields)  \n* **Dynamic** \u2013 cross-service (`audioId` exists, `paletteId` owns user)  \n* **Security** \u2013 depth limit, cost analysis, JWT claims scoping  \n\n### 4.2 REST Fallback\n\n* Code-generated from the GraphQL schema using `gnostic` + custom templates.  \n* Follows HATEOAS, supports `?page[limit]=`, `?page[offset]=` for pagination.  \n\n---\n\n## 5. Versioning Strategy\n\n1. Breaking changes \u2192 new _major_ (e.g., `v2`) schema namespace.  \n2. Additive changes \u2192 patch bump (`v1.3 \u2192 v1.4`) and feature flag.  \n3. Deprecated fields emit `Deprecation-Notice` headers for 90 days.  \n\n```\nquery v1_3 {\n  palette(id: \"ultra-violet\") {          # valid\n    swatches { hex }                     \n  }\n}\n\nquery v2_0 {\n  paletteGet(id: \"ultra-violet\") {       # renamed\n    swatches { hex, rgb }                # new field\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Service Blueprint (C Reference)\n\nA microservice is a standalone **statically-linked** ELF built with **C17** and a thin **gRPC** layer.  \nBelow is a simplified excerpt from `palette_svc/src/service.c`.\n\n```c\n/**\n * @file service.c\n * @brief Palette microservice \u2013 Service entry point & request handlers.\n */\n\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n#include \"core/palette.h\"\n#include \"infra/logger.h\"\n#include \"infra/repository.h\"\n#include \"gen/palette.grpc.pb-c.h\"\n\nstatic palette_repo_t *repo = NULL;\n\n/* gRPC \u2192 C callback ------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic void handle_palette_get(\n        const PaletteGetRequest *req,\n        PaletteGetReply **resp,\n        void *user_data)\n{\n    (void)user_data;\n    sc_trace_span_t span = sc_trace_start(\"palette_get\");\n\n    /* 1. Validate -------------------------------- */\n    if (!req->id || req->id[0] == '\\0') {\n        sc_log_warn(\"palette_get: empty id\");\n        *resp = palette_get_reply__error(\n            HTTP_BAD_REQUEST, \"Palette ID must not be empty\");\n        goto finish;\n    }\n\n    /* 2. Repository ------------------------------ */\n    palette_t pal = {0};\n    sc_error_t err = repo->get(repo, req->id, &pal);\n    if (err.code == SC_ERR_NOT_FOUND) {\n        *resp = palette_get_reply__error(\n            HTTP_NOT_FOUND, \"Palette not found\");\n        goto finish;\n    } else if (err.code != SC_OK) {\n        sc_log_error(\"repo->get failed: %s\", err.msg);\n        *resp = palette_get_reply__error(\n            HTTP_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, \"Internal error\");\n        goto finish;\n    }\n\n    /* 3. Mapping \u2192 ProtoBuf ---------------------- */\n    *resp = palette_get_reply__success(&pal);\n\nfinish:\n    sc_trace_end(&span);\n}\n\nint main(int argc, char **argv)\n{\n    sc_logger_init_default();          /* JSON-structured logs          */\n    sc_trace_init_otel();              /* OpenTelemetry exporter        */\n\n    repo = palette_repo_init(getenv(\"PG_DSN\"));\n    if (!repo) {\n        sc_log_fatal(\"failed to init repository\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    sc_grpc_server_t *srv = sc_grpc_server_create(\"0.0.0.0:7001\");\n    sc_grpc_server_register_palette_get(srv, handle_palette_get, NULL);\n\n    /* Graceful shutdown ------------------------- */\n    signal(SIGTERM, sc_grpc_server_stop);\n    signal(SIGINT,  sc_grpc_server_stop);\n\n    sc_log_info(\"palette_svc listening on :7001\");\n    sc_grpc_server_serve(srv);\n\n    palette_repo_free(repo);\n    sc_grpc_server_free(srv);\n    sc_logger_flush();\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Observability & Monitoring\n\n| Metric                    | Target             | Alert Threshold                    |\n|---------------------------|--------------------|------------------------------------|\n| `http_request_duration`   | < 150 ms p95       | > 250 ms for 5 min                 |\n| `grpc_error_rate`         | < 0.2 %            | > 5 % rolling 1 min                |\n| `redis_cache_hit_ratio`   | > 0.9              | < 0.7 rolling 15 min               |\n| `jetstream_lag`           | < 1 msg           | > 50 msg for 30 s                  |\n\nLogs are shipped to **ELK**, traces to **Jaeger**, metrics scraped by **Prometheus** and rendered in **Grafana** dashboards (`dashboards/` folder).\n\n---\n\n## 8. Security Posture\n\n* **mTLS** between services (`SPIFFE` identities).  \n* **OPA** sidecar on gateway for fine-grained policy.  \n* Every JWT carries:\n  - `cid` (canvas-id) \u2013 tenant sharding\n  - `scopes` \u2013 `palette:rw`, `texture:r`  \n  - `aud` (service audience)  \n\n*Rate limiting* \u2013 token-bucket (Redis) keyed by `sub:cid`.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Failure Modes & Resilience\n\n| Scenario                        | Mitigation                                  |\n|---------------------------------|---------------------------------------------|\n| Network partition               | gRPC retries + circuit-breaker (Hystrix-c)  |\n| Gateway overload                | Adaptive LRU cache, request shedder         |\n| Service crash                   | Kubernetes restart, health probes           |\n| DB connection pool exhaustion   | PgBouncer & slow-query logger               |\n| Upstream incompatible version   | Dual-run old/new schema + feature flags     |\n\n---\n\n## 10. Deployment Pipeline\n\n1. **Pre-merge** \u2013 `clang-tidy`, `cppcheck`, `unit-tests` (CTEST).  \n2. **Build** \u2013 `docker build --platform=linux/amd64 --target runtime`.  \n3. **Security** \u2013 `trivy fs`, SBOM via `syft`.  \n4. **Canary** \u2013 5 % traffic for 30 min, monitored saturation SLOs.  \n5. **Promotion** \u2013 Git tag + Helm release (`charts/`).  \n\n---\n\n## 11. Glossary\n\n| Term       | Meaning                                                    |\n|------------|------------------------------------------------------------|\n| Brush-Stroke | Individual API call altering the live canvas state.       |\n| Swatch       | A semantically-named color token (`#FF22AA`, \u201cultra-violet\u201d). |\n| Texture Node | Procedural fragment generating a 2D/3D texture.          |\n| Narrative Arc| Branch in story graph triggered by user input.           |\n\n---\n\n## 12. References\n\n* _Reactive Design Patterns_ \u2013 R. Kuhn  \n* _Clean Architecture in C_ \u2013 A. Martin  \n* GraphQL Spec `2021-10`  \n* OpenTelemetry v1.26.0  \n\n---\n\n> \u00a9 2024 SynestheticCanvas Consortium \u2013 Released under the Apache 2.0 License\n```",

document is part reference, part living specification.  \n> All code blocks are **production-ready, self-contained C modules** that\n> can be compiled and deployed as-is (barring obvious path changes).  \n> To keep the document future-proof, every sample follows the same\n> conventions you will find across the entire SynestheticCanvas code-base:\n>\n> \u2022 C17 standard  \n> \u2022 No global state except for well-defined singletons  \n> \u2022 `-Wall -Wextra -Werror` clean  \n> \u2022 Strict separation between I/O, domain logic, and data access  \n> \u2022 Independently testable units with graceful shutdown paths  \n\n\n---\n\n## 1  Service Topology\n\n```\n           \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25b6\u2502 Texture  MS  \u2502\n \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25b6\u2502 Audio MS     \u2502\n           \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518          \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                  \u2502\n                  \u25bc\n           \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n           \u2502  API GW      \u2502  (GraphQL+REST, caching, RBAC)\n           \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\nEach micro-service encapsulates exactly one creative concern and  \ncommunicates through HTTP/2 + Protocol Buffers over gRPC *internally*  \nand GraphQL/REST *externally*.\n\n---\n\n## 2  Common Library: `sc_core`\n\nAll services link against a minimal abstraction library that standardises\nlogging, config, tracing, JSON and Protobuf helpers.\n\n```c\n/* File: sc_core/logger.h */\n#ifndef SC_CORE_LOGGER_H\n#define SC_CORE_LOGGER_H\n\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\ntypedef enum {\n    SC_LOG_DEBUG,\n    SC_LOG_INFO,\n    SC_LOG_WARN,\n    SC_LOG_ERROR\n} sc_log_level_t;\n\n/**\n * Initialise the global logger.\n * @param level Minimum level that will be emitted.\n * @return 0 on success, -1 on failure (errno is set).\n */\nint sc_log_init(sc_log_level_t level);\n\n/**\n * Log a formatted message. Always thread-safe.\n */\nvoid sc_log(sc_log_level_t level, const char *fmt, ...);\n\n/* Convenience macros */\n#define SC_LOGD(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_DEBUG, __VA_ARGS__)\n#define SC_LOGI(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_INFO,  __VA_ARGS__)\n#define SC_LOGW(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_WARN,  __VA_ARGS__)\n#define SC_LOGE(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_ERROR, __VA_ARGS__)\n\n#endif /* SC_CORE_LOGGER_H */\n```\n\n```c\n/* File: sc_core/logger.c */\n#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L\n#include \"logger.h\"\n#include <stdarg.h>\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\nstatic struct {\n    sc_log_level_t min_level;\n    pthread_mutex_t mtx;\n    FILE *stream;\n} g_ctx = { .min_level = SC_LOG_INFO, .mtx = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER,\n            .stream = NULL };\n\nstatic const char *level_to_str(sc_log_level_t lvl) {\n    switch (lvl) {\n        case SC_LOG_DEBUG: return \"DEBUG\";\n        case SC_LOG_INFO:  return \"INFO \";\n        case SC_LOG_WARN:  return \"WARN \";\n        default:           return \"ERROR\";\n    }\n}\n\nint sc_log_init(sc_log_level_t level) {\n    g_ctx.min_level = level;\n    g_ctx.stream = stderr;\n    return 0;\n}\n\nvoid sc_log(sc_log_level_t level, const char *fmt, ...) {\n    if (level < g_ctx.min_level) return;\n\n    time_t now = time(NULL);\n    struct tm tm_now;\n    localtime_r(&now, &tm_now);\n\n    char ts[32];\n    strftime(ts, sizeof ts, \"%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S\", &tm_now);\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&g_ctx.mtx);\n    fprintf(g_ctx.stream, \"%s [%s] \", ts, level_to_str(level));\n\n    va_list ap;\n    va_start(ap, fmt);\n    vfprintf(g_ctx.stream, fmt, ap);\n    va_end(ap);\n\n    fputc('\\n', g_ctx.stream);\n    fflush(g_ctx.stream);\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_ctx.mtx);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3  Canonical Service Template\n\nEvery new service clones this template, wires its domain logic, and registers\nwith Consul for discovery.\n\n```c\n/* File: svc_template/main.c */\n#define _DEFAULT_SOURCE\n#include <microhttpd.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include \"router.h\"\n\n#define PORT 8080\n\nstatic volatile sig_atomic_t running = 1;\n\nstatic void handle_sig(int sig) {\n    (void)sig;\n    running = 0;\n}\n\nint main(void) {\n    /* 1. Initialise cross-cutting concerns */\n    sc_log_init(SC_LOG_DEBUG);\n\n    SC_LOGI(\"Starting Palette Service v1.2.0\");\n\n    /* 2. Configure graceful termination */\n    struct sigaction sa = { .sa_handler = handle_sig };\n    sigaction(SIGINT, &sa, NULL);\n    sigaction(SIGTERM, &sa, NULL);\n\n    /* 3. Start HTTP daemon */\n    struct MHD_Daemon *daemon = MHD_start_daemon(\n        MHD_USE_SELECT_INTERNALLY | MHD_USE_EPOLL_INTERNALLY,\n        PORT, NULL, NULL, &router_dispatch, NULL,\n        MHD_OPTION_CONNECTION_TIMEOUT,  (unsigned int)10,\n        MHD_OPTION_END);\n\n    if (!daemon) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"Failed to start HTTP daemon\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    /* 4. Main loop */\n    while (running) {\n        sleep(1);\n    }\n\n    /* 5. Shutdown */\n    MHD_stop_daemon(daemon);\n    SC_LOGI(\"Shutdown complete\");\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```\n\n`router_dispatch` is generated by a compile-time code-gen step that turns an\nOpenAPI spec (`openapi.yaml`) and a GraphQL schema (`schema.graphql`) into a\nmultipart dispatcher.  \nFor brevity, we hand-write a minimal implementation below.\n\n---\n\n## 4  Case Study \u2013 Palette Management Service\n\n### 4.1  Domain Model\n\n```c\n/* File: palette/model.h */\n#ifndef PALETTE_MODEL_H\n#define PALETTE_MODEL_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint32_t id;\n    char     name[64];\n    uint8_t  r, g, b, a;\n} palette_t;\n\n#endif /* PALETTE_MODEL_H */\n```\n\n### 4.2  Repository Layer\n\n```c\n/* File: palette/repository.h */\n#ifndef PALETTE_REPOSITORY_H\n#define PALETTE_REPOSITORY_H\n\n#include \"model.h\"\n#include <stddef.h>\n\n/**\n * Create or update a palette. Returns 0 on success.\n */\nint palette_repo_save(const palette_t *p);\n\n/**\n * Retrieve a palette by ID.\n * @return 0 on success, -ENOENT if not found.\n */\nint palette_repo_get(uint32_t id, palette_t *out);\n\n/**\n * Paginated list of palettes.\n * @param offset Zero-based.\n * @param limit  Max items.\n * @param out    Pre-allocated buffer.\n * @return number of items written, or negative on error.\n */\nssize_t palette_repo_list(size_t offset, size_t limit, palette_t *out);\n\n#endif /* PALETTE_REPOSITORY_H */\n```\n\n```c\n/* File: palette/repository_sqlite.c */\n#define _GNU_SOURCE\n#include \"repository.h\"\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include <sqlite3.h>\n#include <errno.h>\n\nstatic sqlite3 *db = NULL;\n\nstatic int ensure_db(void) {\n    if (db) return 0;\n    int rc = sqlite3_open(\"data/palette.db\", &db);\n    if (rc != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite open error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    char *err = NULL;\n    const char *ddl =\n        \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS palette (\"\n        \"id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,\"\n        \"name TEXT NOT NULL,\"\n        \"r INTEGER NOT NULL,\"\n        \"g INTEGER NOT NULL,\"\n        \"b INTEGER NOT NULL,\"\n        \"a INTEGER NOT NULL);\";\n    rc = sqlite3_exec(db, ddl, NULL, NULL, &err);\n    if (rc != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite DDL error: %s\", err);\n        sqlite3_free(err);\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n\nint palette_repo_save(const palette_t *p) {\n    if (!p) return -EINVAL;\n    if (ensure_db() < 0) return -EIO;\n\n    const char *sql =\n        \"INSERT INTO palette(id, name, r, g, b, a) \"\n        \"VALUES(?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5, ?6) \"\n        \"ON CONFLICT(id) DO UPDATE SET \"\n        \"name=excluded.name, r=excluded.r, g=excluded.g, \"\n        \"b=excluded.b, a=excluded.a;\";\n\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite prepare error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 1, p->id);\n    sqlite3_bind_text  (stmt, 2, p->name, -1, SQLITE_TRANSIENT);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 3, p->r);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 4, p->g);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 5, p->b);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 6, p->a);\n\n    int rc = sqlite3_step(stmt);\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return (rc == SQLITE_DONE) ? 0 : -EIO;\n}\n\nint palette_repo_get(uint32_t id, palette_t *out) {\n    if (!out) return -EINVAL;\n    if (ensure_db() < 0) return -EIO;\n\n    const char *sql = \"SELECT id, name, r, g, b, a FROM palette WHERE id=?1;\";\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite prepare error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    sqlite3_bind_int(stmt, 1, id);\n\n    int rc = sqlite3_step(stmt);\n    if (rc == SQLITE_ROW) {\n        out->id   = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 0);\n        strncpy(out->name, (const char *)sqlite3_column_text(stmt, 1), sizeof out->name);\n        out->r    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 2);\n        out->g    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 3);\n        out->b    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 4);\n        out->a    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 5);\n        sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n        return 0;\n    }\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return -ENOENT;\n}\n\nssize_t palette_repo_list(size_t offset, size_t limit, palette_t *out) {\n    if (!out || !limit) return -EINVAL;\n    if (ensure_db() < 0) return -EIO;\n\n    const char *sql =\n        \"SELECT id, name, r, g, b, a FROM palette \"\n        \"ORDER BY id LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2;\";\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite prepare error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    sqlite3_bind_int(stmt, 1, limit);\n    sqlite3_bind_int(stmt, 2, offset);\n\n    ssize_t count = 0;\n    while (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_ROW && count < (ssize_t)limit) {\n        palette_t *p = &out[count++];\n        p->id = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 0);\n        strncpy(p->name, (const char *)sqlite3_column_text(stmt, 1), sizeof p->name);\n        p->r = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 2);\n        p->g = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 3);\n        p->b = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 4);\n        p->a = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 5);\n    }\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return count;\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3  REST + GraphQL Router\n\n```c\n/* File: svc_template/router.c */\n#include <microhttpd.h>\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include \"palette/repository.h\"\n#include <cjson/cJSON.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\nstatic int json_response(struct MHD_Connection *conn,\n                         const cJSON *json, int status) {\n    char *payload = cJSON_PrintUnformatted(json);\n    struct MHD_Response *resp =\n        MHD_create_response_from_buffer(strlen(payload), payload,\n                                        MHD_RESPMEM_MUST_FREE);\n    if (!resp) return MHD_NO;\n\n    MHD_add_response_header(resp, \"Content-Type\", \"application/json\");\n    int ret = MHD_queue_response(conn, status, resp);\n    MHD_destroy_response(resp);\n    return ret;\n}\n\nstatic int handle_get_palette(struct MHD_Connection *conn,\n                              uint32_t id) {\n    palette_t p;\n    if (palette_repo_get(id, &p) != 0) {\n        cJSON *err = cJSON_CreateObject();\n        cJSON_AddStringToObject(err, \"error\", \"Palette not found\");\n        return json_response(conn, err, MHD_HTTP_NOT_FOUND);\n    }\n\n    cJSON *json = cJSON_CreateObject();\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"id\",   p.id);\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(json, \"name\", p.name);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"r\",    p.r);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"g\",    p.g);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"b\",    p.b);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"a\",    p.a);\n    return json_response(conn, json, MHD_HTTP_OK);\n}\n\nint router_dispatch(void *cls,\n                    struct MHD_Connection *connection,\n                    const char *url, const char *method,\n                    const char *ver, const char *upload_data,\n                    size_t *upload_data_size, void **con_cls) {\n    (void)cls; (void)ver; (void)upload_data; (void)upload_data_size; (void)con_cls;\n\n    SC_LOGD(\"Incoming %s %s\", method, url);\n\n    /* Example route: GET /v1/palette/<id> */\n    if (strcmp(method, \"GET\") == 0 &&\n        strncmp(url, \"/v1/palette/\", 12) == 0) {\n\n        uint32_t id = (uint32_t)strtoul(url + 12, NULL, 10);\n        return handle_get_palette(connection, id);\n    }\n\n    /* Default 404 */\n    cJSON *err = cJSON_CreateObject();\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(err, \"error\", \"Route not found\");\n    return json_response(connection, err, MHD_HTTP_NOT_FOUND);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5  GraphQL Gateway Stub\n\nThe gateway composes service schemas using Apollo Federation syntax\nand delegates sub-queries through the internal gRPC mesh.  \nBelow is a trimmed skeleton that wraps our Palette service.\n\n```c\n/* File: gateway/resolvers/palette_resolver.c */\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include <grpc/grpc.h>\n#include <grpc/byte_buffer.h>\n#include \"generated/palette.grpc.pb-c.h\"\n\nbool gql_resolve_palette(struct gql_query_ctx *ctx) {\n    uint32_t id = gql_arg_u32(ctx, \"id\");\n    Palette__GetRequest req = PALETTE__GET_REQUEST__INIT;\n    req.id = id;\n\n    /* Send over gRPC */\n    grpc_channel *ch = grpc_insecure_channel_create(\"palette:50051\", NULL, NULL);\n    grpc_call *call = grpc_channel_create_call(\n        ch, NULL, GRPC_PROPAGATE_DEFAULT, ctx->cq,\n        grpc_slice_from_static_string(\"/palette.Palette/Get\"),\n        NULL, gpr_inf_future(GPR_CLOCK_REALTIME), NULL);\n\n    grpc_metadata_array md_arr;\n    grpc_metadata_array_init(&md_arr);\n\n    grpc_byte_buffer *payload =\n        grpc_raw_byte_buffer_create(NULL, 0);\n\n    grpc_op ops[6];\n    memset(ops, 0, sizeof ops);\n    ops[0].op = GRPC_OP_SEND_INITIAL_METADATA;\n    ops[0].data.send_initial_metadata.count = 0;\n\n    ops[1].op = GRPC_OP_SEND_MESSAGE;\n    ops[1].data.send_message.send_message = payload;\n\n    ops[2].op = GRPC_OP_SEND_CLOSE_FROM_CLIENT;\n\n    ops[3].op = GRPC_OP_RECV_INITIAL_METADATA;\n    ops[3].data.recv_initial_metadata.recv_initial_metadata = &md_arr;\n\n    grpc_status_code status;\n    grpc_slice details;\n    ops[4].op = GRPC_OP_RECV_STATUS_ON_CLIENT;\n    ops[4].data.recv_status_on_client.status = &status;\n    ops[4].data.recv_status_on_client.status_details = &details;\n\n    grpc_call_error cerr = grpc_call_start_batch(call, ops, 5, NULL, NULL);\n    if (cerr != GRPC_CALL_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"gRPC start batch failed\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    grpc_completion_queue_pluck(ctx->cq, NULL, gpr_inf_future(GPR_CLOCK_REALTIME), NULL);\n\n    /* Transform Protobuf to GraphQL JSON */\n    if (status != GRPC_STATUS_OK) {\n        gql_error(ctx, \"Palette service error\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* Omitted: decode response into ctx->response */\n\n    grpc_metadata_array_destroy(&md_arr);\n    grpc_byte_buffer_destroy(payload);\n    grpc_call_destroy(call);\n    grpc_channel_destroy(ch);\n    return true;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6  Versioning & Lifecycle\n\n- Every service exposes `/version` returning `{ \"semver\": \"x.y.z\", \"git\": \"<sha>\" }`.\n- GraphQL schemas are versioned via `@link(import:)` directives.\n- REST endpoints embed a major version in the URL (`/v1/`, `/v2/`).\n- Obsolete routes remain available for *one* minor version with deprecation\n  warnings in the response headers.\n\n---\n\n## 7  Observability & Resilience\n\n1. **Structured logging** (`JSON` when `LOG_FORMAT=json` env var is set).  \n2. **Metrics** exported via `/metrics` in Prometheus format.  \n3. **Tracing** instrumented through OpenTelemetry C SDK.  \n4. **Circuit-breaker** wrapper auto-generated around every gRPC stub.  \n5. **Rate-limiting** handled at the API Gateway using the Token-Bucket\n   algorithm (Redis backend).\n\n---\n\n## 8  Build & Deployment\n\n```\n$ mkdir build && cd build\n$ cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..\n$ make -j$(nproc)\n$ docker build -t synesthetic/palette:1.2.0 services/palette\n$ helm upgrade --install palette charts/palette\n```\n\nCI jobs run `clang-tidy`, `cppcheck`, unit tests (cmocka), and integration\ntests spun up with `testcontainers-c`.\n\n---\n\n## 9  Appendix \u2013 Compile Flags\n\n```\n-std=c17\n-Wall -Wextra -Werror\n-pedantic\n-fno-common\n-fsanitize=address,undefined\n```\n\n```",

    "content": "```markdown\n# SynestheticCanvas \u2011 API Gateway Architecture  \n*(Module: `api_graphql`)*  \n\n> \u201cTreat every endpoint as a brush stroke.\u201d  \n> \u2014 Lead Architect, SynestheticCanvas\n\n---\n\n## 1. Purpose\n\nThe API Gateway is the single ingress/egress point for **all** client traffic\u2014GraphQL, REST fall-backs, metrics, health checks, and WebSocket subscriptions.  \nIt **does not** implement business logic; it orchestrates:\n\n* Request validation & normalization  \n* Schema version negotiation  \n* Dynamic routing to the appropriate microservice  \n* Response shaping, pagination, and caching  \n* Observability (structured logging, tracing, metrics)  \n* Rate-limiting and traffic shaping  \n\n---\n\n## 2. High-Level Diagram\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    subgraph Gateway\n        A(API Edge) -- gRPC / HTTP --> R[Router]\n        R -- GraphQL --> GQ(GraphQL Engine)\n        R -- REST --> RS(REST Adapter)\n        R -- WS --> WS(WebSocket Hub)\n    end\n\n    GQ -- Async JSON/gRPC --> Microservices\n    RS -- HTTP --> Microservices\n    WS -- Pub/Sub --> Microservices\n\n    Microservices -- gRPC/HTTP --> Datastores[(Data Stores)]\n    subgraph Observability\n        L(Log Aggregator)\n        M(Metrics)\n        T(Tracing)\n    end\n    Gateway -- logs --> L\n    Gateway -- metrics --> M\n    Gateway -- spans --> T\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Technology Stack\n\n| Concern            | Technology / Library                               |\n| ------------------ | -------------------------------------------------- |\n| HTTP / HTTP/2      | [libh2o](https://github.com/h2o/h2o)               |\n| GraphQL Engine     | [cgql](https://github.com/graphql-c/cgql)          |\n| JSON Parsing       | [yyjson](https://github.com/ibireme/yyjson)        |\n| gRPC Client        | [gRPC-C](https://github.com/Juniper/grpc-c)        |\n| WebSocket          | Built-in H2O WS API                                |\n| Caching            | pluggable: Redis, in-process LRU                   |\n| Metrics            | [Prometheus-C](https://github.com/digitalocean/prometheus-client-c)|\n| Tracing            | OpenTelemetry C SDK                                |\n| Logging            | [spdlog-c](https://github.com/irsl/spdlog-c)       |\n\n> All third-party dependencies are vendored and version-pinned via `cmake/FetchContent` to ensure reproducibility.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Request Life-Cycle\n\n1. **Ingress**  \n   \u2013 `libh2o` accepts the TCP/TLS connection and performs ALPN (HTTP/2, HTTP/1.1, WebSocket).  \n2. **Pre-flight Filters**  \n   \u2013 IP allow/deny, rate limiter, TLS client-certificate check.  \n3. **Protocol Router**  \n   \u2013 Based on `:path` and `Content-Type` headers:  \n     * `/graphql` \u2192 GraphQL handler  \n     * `/v{N}/**`  \u2192 REST adapter (versioned)  \n     * `/ws`       \u2192 WebSocket Hub  \n4. **Validation**  \n   \u2013 JSON Schema (REST) or GraphQL AST validation, depth-limit, complexity analyzer.  \n5. **Service Discovery**  \n   \u2013 Resolve microservice target via Consul or static registry.  \n6. **Proxy / Execution**  \n   \u2013 Forward the request (gRPC or HTTP).  \n   \u2013 Collect partial responses for **federated** GraphQL queries.  \n7. **Response Filters**  \n   \u2013 Pagination, error redaction, ETag/caching headers.  \n   \u2013 Observability emit (metrics, traces).  \n8. **Egress**  \n   \u2013 Send response, close connection if needed.  \n\n---\n\n## 5. Key Design Decisions\n\n### 5.1 Versioned GraphQL Schemas\n\nSchemas are **append-only**; breaking changes require a new major (`v2`, `v3`, \u2026).  \nGateway negotiates version through:\n\n1. `X-SC-GraphQL-Schema: vN` header (preferred)  \n2. `SC-GQL-Schema` cookie (Web clients)  \n3. Fallback to the greatest supported version.  \n\n### 5.2 REST as a Compatibility Layer\n\nEvery GraphQL field with `@rest` directive automatically spawns a REST endpoint during build:\n\n```graphql\ntype Palette {\n    id: ID!\n    name: String! @rest(path: \"/v1/palettes/{id}\", method: GET)\n    colors: [Color!]!\n}\n```\n\nThe code-gen step creates a fa\u00e7ade function in `rest_adapter.c` that marshals to the GraphQL resolver internally (see \u00a76).\n\n---\n\n## 6. Core Source Walk-through\n\nBelow are trimmed but **compilable** excerpts that illustrate best practices.\n\n### 6.1 gateway.c \u2013 Entry Point\n\n```c\n/**\n * gateway.c\n * ----------\n * SynestheticCanvas API Gateway entry point.\n * Bootstraps the web server, loads plugin modules, \n * and wires observability hooks.\n */\n#include <h2o.h>\n#include <cgql/cgql.h>\n#include <yyjson.h>\n#include <prom.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n\n#include \"config.h\"\n#include \"router.h\"\n#include \"observability.h\"\n\nstatic h2o_globalconf_t   g_config;\nstatic h2o_context_t      g_ctx;\nstatic h2o_multithread_queue_t *g_queue = NULL;\n\nstatic void on_sigterm(int signo) {\n    h2o_context_request_shutdown(&g_ctx);\n}\n\nint main(int argc, char **argv)\n{\n    // 1. Parse CLI / ENV configuration\n    sc_config_t cfg = {0};\n    if (sc_config_load(&cfg, argc, argv) != 0) {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"Failed to load configuration\\n\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Initialize logging ASAP\n    sc_log_init(cfg.log_level, cfg.log_file);\n\n    // 3. Observability stack\n    if (sc_observe_init(&cfg.observe) != 0) {\n        SC_LOG_ERROR(\"Observability init failed\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    // 4. Setup H2O global configuration\n    h2o_config_init(&g_config);\n    sc_router_register(&g_config, &cfg);\n\n    // 5. Create listener sockets\n    int listener_fd = sc_socket_create_listener(cfg.bind_address, cfg.port);\n    if (listener_fd < 0) {\n        SC_LOG_ERROR(\"Cannot bind %s:%d\", cfg.bind_address, cfg.port);\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    // 6. Initialize thread pool\n    h2o_context_init(&g_ctx, h2o_evloop_create(), &g_config);\n    g_queue = h2o_multithread_create_queue(&g_ctx, \"sc-queue\");\n\n    // 7. Signal handling\n    signal(SIGTERM, on_sigterm);\n    signal(SIGINT,  on_sigterm);\n\n    SC_LOG_INFO(\"SynestheticCanvas Gateway started on %s:%d\", \n                cfg.bind_address, cfg.port);\n\n    // 8. Main event loop\n    while (h2o_evloop_run(g_ctx.loop, INT32_MAX) == 0);\n\n    // 9. Graceful shutdown\n    h2o_context_dispose(&g_ctx);\n    h2o_config_dispose(&g_config);\n    sc_observe_shutdown();\n    sc_config_free(&cfg);\n\n    SC_LOG_INFO(\"Gateway shut down gracefully\");\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```\n\n### 6.2 router.c \u2013 URL Multiplexer\n\n```c\n/**\n * router.c\n * --------\n * Declarative URL routing. New routes are appended\n * here by code-gen scripts to avoid scattered logic.\n */\n#include \"router.h\"\n#include \"handlers/graphql_handler.h\"\n#include \"handlers/rest_handler.h\"\n#include \"handlers/ws_handler.h\"\n\nvoid sc_router_register(h2o_globalconf_t *glob, const sc_config_t *cfg)\n{\n    h2o_pathconf_t *graphql  = h2o_config_register_path(glob, \"/graphql\", 0);\n    graphql->handlers = (h2o_handler_t *[]){\n        sc_graphql_handler_create(glob, cfg), NULL\n    };\n\n    h2o_pathconf_t *rest_v1  = h2o_config_register_path(glob, \"/v1\", H2O_URL_EGL_LIKELY);\n    rest_v1->handlers = (h2o_handler_t *[]){\n        sc_rest_handler_create(glob, cfg, 1), NULL\n    };\n\n    h2o_pathconf_t *rest_v2  = h2o_config_register_path(glob, \"/v2\", 0);\n    rest_v2->handlers = (h2o_handler_t *[]){\n        sc_rest_handler_create(glob, cfg, 2), NULL\n    };\n\n    h2o_pathconf_t *ws       = h2o_config_register_path(glob, \"/ws\", 0);\n    ws->handlers = (h2o_handler_t *[]){\n        sc_ws_handler_create(glob, cfg), NULL\n    };\n}\n```\n\n### 6.3 graphql_handler.c \u2013 Streaming Execution\n\n```c\n/**\n * GraphQL Handler\n */\n#include <cgql/executor.h>\n#include <cgql/validator.h>\n#include \"handlers/graphql_handler.h\"\n#include \"services/federation.h\"\n\ntypedef struct {\n    h2o_handler_t super;\n    sc_config_t  *cfg;\n} sc_graphql_handler_t;\n\nstatic int on_req(h2o_handler_t *self, h2o_req_t *req)\n{\n    sc_graphql_handler_t *h = (sc_graphql_handler_t *)self;\n\n    // 1. Ensure method POST\n    if (req->method.len != 4 || memcmp(req->method.base, \"POST\", 4) != 0) {\n        return h2o_send_error_405(req, \"Method Not Allowed\", \"\", H2O_SEND_ERROR_KEEP_HEADERS);\n    }\n\n    // 2. Parse JSON body\n    yyjson_doc *doc = NULL;\n    if (sc_json_parse_request(req, &doc) != 0) {\n        return h2o_send_error_400(req, \"Invalid JSON\", \"\", 0);\n    }\n\n    // 3. Extract \"query\" and \"variables\"\n    const char *query     = sc_json_get_string(doc, \"query\");\n    yyjson_val *vars_node = yyjson_get(doc, \"variables\");\n\n    // 4. Parse & validate GraphQL\n    cgql_parser_t *parser = cgql_parser_new(query);\n    cgql_ast_t    *ast    = cgql_parse(parser);\n\n    if (!ast) {\n        sc_json_free(doc);\n        cgql_parser_free(parser);\n        return h2o_send_error_400(req, \"GraphQL parse error\", parser->last_error, 0);\n    }\n\n    char *validation_err = NULL;\n    if (!cgql_validate(ast, &validation_err)) {\n        sc_json_free(doc);\n        cgql_ast_free(ast);\n        cgql_parser_free(parser);\n        int res = h2o_send_error_400(req, \"GraphQL validation error\", \n                                     validation_err, 0);\n        free(validation_err);\n        return res;\n    }\n\n    // 5. Execute against federated services\n    yyjson_mut_doc *result = sc_fed_execute(h->cfg, ast, vars_node);\n\n    // 6. Serialize response\n    sc_http_send_json(req, result);\n\n    // Cleanup\n    sc_json_free(doc);\n    yyjson_mut_doc_free(result);\n    cgql_ast_free(ast);\n    cgql_parser_free(parser);\n    return 0;\n}\n\nh2o_handler_t *sc_graphql_handler_create(h2o_globalconf_t *glob, const sc_config_t *cfg)\n{\n    sc_graphql_handler_t *h = h2o_mem_alloc_shared(NULL, sizeof(*h), NULL);\n    h2o_handler_init((h2o_handler_t *)h, sizeof(*h));\n    h->super.on_req = on_req;\n    h->cfg          = (sc_config_t *)cfg;\n    return (h2o_handler_t *)h;\n}\n```\n\n### 6.4 rest_adapter.c \u2013 Auto-Generated Example\n\n```c\n/**\n * Auto-generated REST endpoint for Palette retrieval.\n * Mirrors the GraphQL field: Palette.name\n */\n#include \"handlers/rest_handler.h\"\n#include \"proto/palette.pb-c.h\"\n#include \"services/palette_client.h\"\n\nstatic int handle_get_palette(h2o_handler_t *self, h2o_req_t *req)\n{\n    const h2o_iovec_t *id = h2o_req_extract_path_param(req, \"id\");\n    if (!id || id->len == 0) {\n        return h2o_send_error_400(req, \"Missing palette id\", \"\", 0);\n    }\n\n    PaletteRequest pr = PALETTE_REQUEST__INIT;\n    pr.id = strndup(id->base, id->len);\n\n    PaletteResponse *resp = palette_client_get(&pr);\n    free(pr.id);\n\n    if (!resp) {\n        return h2o_send_error_502(req, \"Upstream failure\", \"\", 0);\n    }\n\n    yyjson_mut_doc *doc = yyjson_mut_doc_new(NULL);\n    yyjson_mut_obj_add_str(doc, doc, \"id\", resp->id);\n    yyjson_mut_obj_add_str(doc, doc, \"name\", resp->name);\n\n    sc_http_send_json(req, doc);\n    palette_response__free_unpacked(resp, NULL);\n    yyjson_mut_doc_free(doc);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Observability Blueprint\n\n1. **Structured Logging** \u2192 JSON lines,  `stderr` fallback.  \n2. **Metrics** \u2192 Prometheus exposition `/metrics`.  \n3. **Tracing** \u2192 OpenTelemetry exporter (Jaeger by default).  \n4. **Health** \u2192 `GET /healthz` (liveness) and `/readyz` (readiness).  \n\nExample Prometheus metric naming:\n\n```text\nsc_gateway_request_total{method=\"POST\",endpoint=\"/graphql\",status=\"2xx\"} 135\nsc_gateway_upstream_latency_seconds_bucket{service=\"texture_svc\",le=\"0.1\"} 512\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Resilience & Scaling\n\n* **Circuit Breakers:** Per-service rolling window on failure rate.  \n* **Rate Limiting:** Token bucket via Redis or in-mem fallback.  \n* **Autoscaling Signals:** P95 latency, CPU, custom \u201cbrush_stroke\u201d metric.  \n* **Blue/Green Deploy:** Canary header `X-SC-Canary: true`.  \n\n---\n\n## 9. Future Work\n\n* GraphQL defer/stream support (incremental delivery)  \n* WASM plugin sandbox for user-defined resolvers  \n* QUIC/HTTP-3 transport evaluation  \n\n---\n\n## 10. References\n\n* \u201cBuilding an API Gateway in C\u201d, *C90Con* (2022).  \n* \u201cGraphQL Federation at Scale\u201d, *FOSDEM* (2023).  \n\n---\n\n> **Document ID:** `SC-ARCH-APIGW`  \n> **Last Reviewed:** 2024-05-09  \n> **Maintainers:** `@infra-paint`, `@canvas-ops`\n\n```",

atomic_init(&cli->requests_total, 0);\n    atomic_init(&cli->failures_total, 0);\n\n    if (pthread_mutex_init(&cli->curl_mtx, NULL) != 0)\n    {\n        LOG_ERR(\"Failed to init mutex: %s\", strerror(errno));\n        free(cli);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (curl_global_init(CURL_GLOBAL_ALL) != CURLE_OK)\n    {\n        LOG_ERR(\"Failed to init libcurl\");\n LOG_ERR(\"curl_easy_init() failed\");\n        curl_global_cleanup();\n        pthread_mutex_destroy(&cli->curl_mtx);\n        free(cli);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Use connection pooling */\n    curl_easy_setopt(cli->curl_handle, CURLOPT_DNS_CACHE_TIMEOUT, 60L);\n\n    LOG_INF(\"Service client initialised\");\n    return cli;\n}\n\nvoid sc_service_client_free(sc_service_client_t *cli)\n{\n    if (!cli) return;\n\n    LOG_INF(\"Releasing service client (totalRequests=%\" PRIu64 \", failures=%\" PRIu64 \")\",\n            atomic_load(&cli->requests_total), atomic_load(&cli->failures_total));\n\n    free(cli->palette_url);\n    free(cli->texture_url);\n    free(cli->audio_url);\n    free(cli->narrative_url);\n\n    if (cli->curl_handle) curl_easy_cleanup(cli->curl_handle);\n    curl_global_cleanup();\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&cli->curl_mtx);\n    free(cli);\n}\n\nint sc_service_client_call(sc_service_client_t *cli,\n                           sc_service_endp_t    endpoint,\n                           const char          *method,\n                           const char          *path,\n                           const char          *request_json,\n                           cJSON              **response_json,\n                           long                *http_status)\n{\n    if (!cli || !method || !path || !http_status)\n        return SC_EINVAL;\n\n    char *full_url = build_full_url(endpoint, cli, path);\n    if (!full_url)\n        return SC_EINVAL;\n\n    atomic_fetch_add_explicit(&cli->requests_total, 1, memory_order_relaxed);\n\n    int rc = perform_request(cli, full_url, method, request_json, http_status, response_json);\n    free(full_url);\n\n    if (rc != SC_OK)\n        atomic_fetch_add_explicit(&cli->failures_total, 1, memory_order_relaxed);\n\n    return rc;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Private Implementation\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic char *build_full_url(sc_service_endp_t ep, sc_service_client_t *client, const char *path)\n{\n    const char *base = NULL;\n    switch (ep)\n    {\n        case SC_EP_PALETTE:   base = client->palette_url;   break;\n        case SC_EP_TEXTURE:   base = client->texture_url;   break;\n        case SC_EP_AUDIO:     base = client->audio_url;     break;\n        case SC_EP_NARRATIVE: base = client->narrative_url; break;\n        default: return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (!base)\n    {\n        LOG_ERR(\"Endpoint base URL not configured\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    size_t needed = strlen(base) + strlen(path) + 2; /* '/' + '\\0' */\n    char *url = malloc(needed);\n    if (!url) -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                Validators                                  */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* Validate a UUID argument (simple length/format check). */\nstatic int validate_uuid_arg(const char *uuid, GQLError **gql_err)\n{\n    /* Very permissive validation; can be swapped for libcork or libuuid */\n    if (!uuid || strlen(uuid) != 36) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_VALIDATION, \"Invalid UUID\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* Extract and validate pagination arguments. */\nstatic int extract_pagination(const json_t *args,\n                              size_t *out_first,\n                              const char **out_after,\n                              GQLError **gql_err)\n{\n    json_t *first_json = json_object_get(args, \"first\");\n    json_t *after_json = json_object_get(args, \"after\");\n\n    if (first_json && !json_is_integer(first_json)) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_VALIDATION, \"`first` must be an integer\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    if (after_json && !json_is_string(after_json)) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_VALIDATION, \"`after` must be a string cursor\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    if (first_json) *out_first = (size_t)json_integer_value(first_json);\n    if (after_json) *out_after = json_string_value(after_json);\n\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                          Resolver implementations                          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * palette(id: ID!): Palette!\n */\nstatic json_t *resolve_palette(const json_t *args, void *user_data, GQLError **gql_err)\n{\n    gql_context_t *ctx = (gql_context_t *)user_data;\n\n    const char *id = json_string_value(json_object_get(args, \"id\"));\n    if (validate_uuid_arg(id, gql_err) < 0) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Throttle upstream calls */\n    if (rate_limiter_acquire(ctx->limiter) != 0) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_RATE_LIMIT, \"Too many requests\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    char url[512];\n    snprintf(url, sizeof(url), \"%s/palettes/%s\", PALETTE_SERVICE_BASE_URL, id);\n\n    LOG_INFO(ctx->log, \"GET %s\", url);\n    json_t *payload = http_json_get(url, ctx->log, gql_err);\n    if (!payload) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    METRIC_INC(ctx->metrics, \"palette_resolver_success\");\n    return payload; /* Ownership transferred to GraphQL runtime */\n}\n\n/**\n * palettes(first: Int, after: String): PaletteConnection!\n */\nstatic json_t *resolve_palettes(const json_t *args, void *user_data, GQLError **gql_err)\n{\n    gql_context_t *ctx = (gql_context_t *)user_data;\n\n    size_t first       = 25; /* default page size */\n    const char *after  = NULL;\n\n    if (extract_pagination(args, &first, &after, gql_err) < 0) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (first == 0 || first > 100) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_VALIDATION, \"`first` must be between 1 and 100\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Construct query string */\n    char url[512];\n    if (after) {\n        snprintf(url, sizeof(url),\n                 \"%s/palettes?limit=%zu&cursor=%s\", PALETTE_SERVICE_BASE_URL, first, after);\n    } else {\n        snprintf(url, sizeof(url),\n                 \"%s/palettes?limit=%zu\", PALETTE_SERVICE_BASE_URL, first);\n    }\n\n    LOG_INFO(ctx->log, \"GET %s\", url);\n    json_t *payload = http_json_get(url, ctx->log, gql_err);\n    if (!payload) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    METRIC_INC(ctx->metrics, \"palettes_resolver_success\");\n    return payload;\n}\n\n/**\n * createPalette(input: CreatePaletteInput!): Palette!\n *\n * For simplicity, we forward the entire JSON payload to the palette service.\n */\nstatic json_t *resolve_create_palette(const json_t *args, void *user_data, GQLError **gql_err)\n{\n    gql_context_t *ctx = (gql_context_t *)user_data;\n\n    /* Rate limiting */\n    if (rate_limiter_acquire(ctx->limiter) != 0) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_RATE_LIMIT, \"Too many requests\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Validate mandatory fields */\n    const json_t *input = json_object_get(args, \"input\");\n    if (!input || !json_is_object(input)) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_VALIDATION, \"`input` must be provided\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    const char *name = json_string_value(json_object_get(input, \"name\"));\n    if (!name || strlen(name) == 0) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_VALIDATION, \"`name` cannot be empty\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Serialize input to JSON for POST body */\n    char *body = json_dumps(input, JSON_COMPACT);\n    if (!body) {\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_INTERNAL, \"JSON serialization failed\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Prepare CURL */\n    CURL *curl = curl_easy_init();\n    if (!curl) {\n        free(body);\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_INTERNAL, \"Internal HTTP init error\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    char url[512];\n    snprintf(url, sizeof(url), \"%s/palettes\", PALETTE_SERVICE_BASE_URL);\n\n    struct curl_slist *headers = NULL;\n    headers = curl_slist_append(headers, \"Content-Type: application/json\");\n\n    curl_buffer_t chunk = {.data = NULL, .size = 0};\n\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_URL, url);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POST, 1L);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, headers);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS, body);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDSIZE, (long)strlen(body));\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, curl_buffer_write);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, (void *)&chunk);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_TIMEOUT, HTTP_TIMEOUT_SECS);\n\n    LOG_INFO(ctx->log, \"POST %s\", url);\n    CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(curl);\n    long http_status = 0;\n    curl_easy_getinfo(curl, CURLINFO_RESPONSE_CODE, &http_status);\n\n    curl_easy_cleanup(curl);\n    curl_slist_free_all(headers);\n    free(body);\n\n    if (res != CURLE_OK) {\n        LOG_ERROR(ctx->log, \"curl_easy_perform() failed: %s\", curl_easy_strerror(res));\n        free(chunk.data);\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_NETWORK, \"Upstream network error\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (http_status >= 400) {\n        LOG_WARN(ctx->log, \"Upstream error %ld for POST %s\", http_status, url);\n        free(chunk.data);\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_UPSTREAM, \"Upstream service error\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    json_error_t json_err;\n    json_t *json = json_loads(chunk.data, 0, &json_err);\n    free(chunk.data);\n\n    if (!json) {\n        LOG_ERROR(ctx->log, \"JSON parse error at line %d: %s\", json_err.line, json_err.text);\n        *gql_err = gql_error_new(GQL_ERR_INTERNAL, \"Invalid upstream JSON\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    METRIC_INC(ctx->metrics, \"create_palette_resolver_success\");\n    return json;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           Registration / bootstrap                         */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * gql_register_resolvers:\n *\n * Register all resolvers for the palette sub-graph with the GraphQL runtime.\n */\nint gql_register_resolvers(GraphQLRuntime *runtime,\n                           logger_t *log,\n                           metrics_t *metrics,\n                           rate_limiter_t *limiter)\n{\n    if (!runtime) return -EINVAL;\n\n    gql_context_t *ctx = calloc(1, sizeof(*ctx));\n    if (!ctx) {\n        LOG_ERROR(log, \"Out of memory allocating gql_context_t\");\n        return -ENOMEM;\n    }\n\n    ctx->log     = log;\n    ctx->metrics = metrics;\n    ctx->limiter = limiter;\n\n    int rc = 0;\n\n    rc |= graphql_register_resolver(runtime, \"Query\",  \"palette\",\n                                    resolve_palette,       ctx /*user_data*/);\n\n    rc |= graphql_register_resolver(runtime, \"Query\",  \"palettes\",\n                                    resolve_palettes,      ctx);\n\n    rc |= graphql_register_resolver(runtime, \"Mutation\",\"createPalette\",\n                                    resolve_create_palette, ctx);\n\n    if (rc != 0) {\n        LOG_ERROR(log, \"Failed to register one or more GraphQL resolvers\");\n        free(ctx);\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    LOG_INFO(log, \"Palette resolvers registered successfully\");\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           Graceful shutdown hook                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nvoid gql_resolvers_shutdown(GraphQLRuntime *runtime)\n{\n    /* Currently nothing to free. Add schema-wide cleanup here if needed. */\n    (void)runtime;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                   EOF                                      */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n",
